1935.11.03

Sixth Plenary Session: First General Meeting Held Yesterday 1

Decisions Made on Committee Members for Examining Various Proposals; Telegram Urges Central Committee Members from Guangdong and Guangxi to Come to Beijing Immediately; Ye Chu-cang Requests Punishment for Himself, No Discussion Needed; Establishment of Committee to Review Draft Constitution

(Nanjing) The Sixth Plenary Session held its first general meeting at 9:00 AM on the 2nd. Executive committee members present included Chiang Kai-shek, Sun Ke, Tai Chuan-hsien, He Yingqin, Chen Guofu, Ye Chu-cang, Zhu Peide, Yu Youren, He Chengjun, Wang Boling, Shao Yuanchong, Zhu Jiahua, Zhou Qigang, Zhang Qun, Chen Lifu, Chen Zhaoying, Zeng Yangfu, Fang Juehui, Wang Boqun, Li Wenfan, Yan Xishan, Feng Yuxiang, Li Liejun, Bo Wenwei, Qin Zhen, Wang Faqin, Chen Gongbo, Cheng Qian, Jing Hengyi, Gan Naiguang, Ju Zheng, Shi Ying, Liu Shouchong, Ding Chaowu, Zhang Zhen, Wang Zhengting, Zhou Fo Hai, Xia Douyin, Yang Jie, Gui Chongji, Ma Chaojun, Chen Ce, Deng Jiayan, Mao Zuquan, Li Zonghuang, Bai Yunti, Zhang Zhiben, Fu Rulin, and others, totaling 47 individuals. Alternate executive committee members present included Zhu Jiqing, Miao Bin, Zhao Pilian, Yu Jingtang, Xue Dubi, Jiao Yitang, Miao Peicheng, Ke Xing'e, Xiao Jishan, Zhan Jusi, Xie Zuomin, Huang Jilu, Liang Hancao, Qian Dajun, Guan Suren, Duan Xipeng, Li Renren, Zheng Zhannan, Cui Guangxiu, Zhang Lisheng, Huang Fusheng, Luo Jialun, Zhang Dingfan, Dai Kuisheng, Li Jingzhai, Wang Qi, Fan Yusui, Zeng Kuoqing, Wang Maogong, Tang Shengzhi, Chen Qingyun, Tang Youren, Wang Luyi, and others, totaling 32 individuals. Supervisory committee members present included Wu Jingheng, Zhang Renjie, Lin Sen, Cai Yuanpei, Zhang Ji, Shao Lizi, Li Yuying, Liu Yazi, Zhang Xueliang, Yang Hu, Hong Ludong, Xu Chongzhi, Zhang Fakui, and others, totaling 13 individuals. Alternate supervisory committee members present included Huang Shaoxiong, Guo Chuntao, Li Fulin, Chen Bulei, Deng Qingyang, Li Qian, Deng Feihuang, Sun Jingya, Xiao Zhongzhen, Ji Liang, Li Ciwen, and others, totaling 11 individuals. Ju Zheng chaired the meeting.

Reported Matters: (1) Reading of the minutes of the preparatory meeting; (2) Secretary-General's report on documents: 1. Two letters and telegrams from committee members; 2. Nineteen congratulatory telegrams; (3) Presidium Report: 1. Decision on the list of committee members for various proposal review groups; 2. Decision to send a telegram to the Central Committee members in Guangdong and Guangxi, reporting on the assassination attempt on Mr. Wang and requesting all committee members, for both public and private reasons, to come to Beijing immediately; 3. Telegrams to Hu Hanmin and Wang Chonghui, reporting on the assassination attempt on Mr. Wang; 4. Secretary-General Ye, also chairman of the Publicity Committee, requested punishment for himself due to the attack and injury of Wang, a committee member, by an assassin within the Party organs. The assembly requested that Ye resume his duties, and the requested punishment should not be discussed; (4) Party affairs report submitted to the Party Affairs Group for review; (5) Political report; (6) Executive Yuan report; (7) Legislative Yuan report; (8) Judicial Yuan report; (9) Examination Yuan report; (10) Control Yuan report, all submitted to the Political Group for review.

Matters for Discussion: (1) The Draft Constitution of the Republic of China. After statements by committee members Li Liejun, Shao Yuanchong, and Zhang Qun, it was resolved to establish a committee to review the Draft Constitution of the Republic of China. The following were designated as conveners: Ju Zheng, Zhang Ji, Sun Ke, committee members Xu Chongzhi, Chen Lifu, Fang Juehui, Wang Faqin, Ma Chaojun, Bai Yunti, Zeng Kuoqing, Gu Zhenggang, Wang Luyi, Zhan Jusi, Feng Yuxiang, Zhang Qun, Liu Zhi, Chen Zhaoying, Qin Zhen, Gan Naiguang, Deng Jiayan, Jiao Yitang, Mao Zuquan Zhang Ji, Huang Shaoxiong, Zhang Zhiben, Sun Jingya, Li Zonghuang, Huang Jilu, Shao Lizi, Gu Mengyu, He Yingqin, Zhang Xueliang, Bo Wenwei, Zhang Dingfan, Cheng Qian, Zhang Fakui, Yan Xishan, Li Liejun, Dai Chuanbao, Ye Chu-cang, Zhang Lisheng. Gui Chongji. Shao Yuanchong, Wang Zhengting, Chen Gongbo, Fu Rulin, Zhang Daofan, Tang Youren. Wu Tiecheng, Xue Dubi. Li Wenfan, Kong Xiangxi, Shi Ying, Zhou Fo Hai. Ke Xing'e, Luo Jialun, Chen Bulei, Cai Yuanpei, Wu Jingheng, Li Yuying, Liang Hancao. Participants: Wang Shijie, Fu Bingchang, Wu Jingxiong, Lin Bin. Secretary Tao Luqian. (Central News Agency dispatch, 2nd)

List of Committee Members for Various Review Groups

(Nanjing) The Presidium's report designates the following list of committee members for the proposal review groups: Party Affairs Group: Xu Chongzhi, Chen Lifu, Zhan Jusi, Cui Guangxiu, and others, totaling 25 individuals. Conveners: Wang Faqin, Chen Guofu. Political Group: Feng Yuxiang, Zhang Qun, Liu Zhi, Shao Lizi, Gu Mengyu, and others, totaling 21 individuals. Conveners: Zhang Ji, Huang Shaoxiong. Military Group: He Yingqin, Zhu Peide, Zhang Xueliang, Tang Shengzhi, Zhang Fakui Yan Xishan, Li Liejun, and others, totaling 22 individuals. Conveners: Yan Xishan, He Yingqin. Economic Group: Shao Yuanchong, Wang Zhengting, Xue Dubi, Guan Suren, and others, totaling 20 individuals. Conveners: Kong Xiangxi, Li Wenfan. Education Group: Shi Ying, Zhu Jiahua, Chen Bulei, and others, totaling 20 individuals. Conveners: Cai Yuanpei, Wu Jingheng. (Central News Agency dispatch, 2nd)

Memorial Week Scheduled for the 4th

(Nanjing) The Sixth Plenary Session has scheduled a Memorial Week to be held at 8:00 AM on the 4th, with Yu Youren designated as the chairman and Cai Yuanpei to deliver a report. All Central Committee members are notified to attend. The seating arrangement for Central Committee members will be based on age, with Central Committee members over 60 years of age in the first row, those over 50 in the second row, those over 40 in the next row, and those under 40 in the back, to ensure order. (Central News Agency dispatch, 2nd)

Various Review Groups Hold Separate Meetings

(Nanjing) The Sixth Plenary Session held review meetings in the afternoon of the 2nd. All four groups—Party Affairs, Political, Economic, and Education—held separate meetings, except for the Military Group. The meetings were chaired by their respective conveners. The Party Affairs Group adjourned relatively late, and the cases under review were drafted into reports and submitted to the Presidium for presentation to the general meeting. (Central News Agency dispatch, 2nd)

Feng Yuxiang Meets with Chiang for a Long Talk

(Nanjing) Feng Yuxiang entered the city from the mausoleum at 7:00 AM on the 2nd and visited He Yingqin, Zhang Ji, Qin Zhen, Li Liejun, and others to express his gratitude and engage in discussions. He then attended the plenary session. At noon, he met with Chiang for a long conversation and stayed at Chiang's residence for lunch. (Special dispatch, 2nd)

After Telegram of Wang's Assassination Arrives, Guangdong Side Holds All-Night Meeting 2

(Hong Kong) After the telegram of the assassination attempt on Wang arrived in Guangdong, the political affairs committee held a meeting at noon to discuss the matter. Later that night, committee members went to Chen Jitang's residence for a talk that lasted until 1:00 AM. Chen Jitang and Li Zongren recently telegraphed Bai Chongxi in Nanning, inviting him to Guangdong. Bai plans to go east on the 10th. (2nd Dispatch)

(Hong Kong) Li Yangjing returned to the province from Dongguan on the 2nd. (2nd Dispatch)

Suma Returns to Nanjing by Plane 3

(Beiping) Suma, the Japanese Consul-General stationed in Beijing, came to Beiping from Tianjin a few days ago for sightseeing. He flew back to Nanjing by China Aviation plane at 7:00 AM on the 2nd. Also, Matsui went to Tianjin on the morning of the 2nd to visit Tada. (Central News Agency dispatch, 2nd)

(Nanjing) A certain Japanese newspaper in Shanghai published a dispatch from Nanjing on the 31st stating that Vice Foreign Minister Tang visited Japanese Consul-General Suma early that morning, etc., in a lengthy news article. According to reliable sources, this report is completely fabricated. Not only did Vice Foreign Minister Tang not meet with any foreign guests that morning, but Consul-General Suma had not yet returned to Nanjing that day, making a meeting impossible. (Central News Agency dispatch, 2nd)

Premier Wang's Condition Good After Treatment 4

Slept Comfortably, Temperature and Pulse Same as Normal; Bullet Lodged in Rib Space, No Inflammation as of Yesterday; Assassin Sun Fengming Dies from Severe Wounds

(Nanjing) Wang's condition has been good after being admitted to the hospital. According to doctors, if there are no special changes in the next two days, his safety can be assured. On the 2nd, he consumed milk and orange juice four times. In the morning, he asked for a copy of the Central Daily News and briefly browsed through it. He was then persuaded by the doctor to rest, and Wang's wife read to him. (Special dispatch, 2nd)

(Nanjing) Premier Wang underwent surgery at 4:00 PM on the 1st under local anesthesia to remove several bone fragments and small shrapnel from his left cheek. The wound on his back was cleaned and sutured. He slept comfortably that night. This morning, his temperature was 37.5 degrees Celsius, pulse was 82, and respiration was 18. Dr. Branch, a physician from Shanghai, arrived in Nanjing early on the 2nd to consult with Liu Ruiheng and Shen Kefei. They jointly announced that Premier Wang's injuries were not serious and his condition was good. (Special dispatch, 2nd)

(Nanjing) Premier Wang's wound on his left cheek was bandaged twice on the 2nd. At 4:00 PM, he received an intramuscular injection of 500 units of tetanus antitoxin serum. This injection is a routine procedure in the hospital for anyone who has suffered a gunshot wound to prevent any possible tetanus infection. His temperature was 37.4, pulse 80, and respiration 16. His condition is progressing well. (Special dispatch, 2nd)

Central Hospital Reports on Patient's Condition

(Nanjing) As of 10:00 AM on the 2nd, 24 hours had passed since Premier Wang was attacked, and his treatment has been progressing very well. According to Central Hospital's announcement at 11:00 AM on the 2nd, Wang's temperature this morning was 37.5 degrees, a slight decrease from yesterday; his pulse was 82, and his respiration was 18, both within normal range. He slept very well on the night of the 1st, so his spirits were even better this morning. He spoke normally and maintained a stable demeanor. This morning, he consumed milk, chicken soup, and orange juice. After the meal, he requested to read the newspaper. Because the doctor ordered him not to overwork, the Central Daily News was presented to him, and Wang briefly read it before Chen Bijun read aloud various important news items. Wang was quite pleased after listening. The redness and swelling on his left cheek had slightly subsided, the skin wound on his left arm had scabbed over, and the bullet in the rib space on his back showed no signs of inflammation as of 10:00 AM on the 2nd. At 8:00 AM on the 2nd, Chairman Lin and Chairman Chiang visited the hospital to express their concern in person. Zhang Jingjiang, Wu Zhihui, Li Shizeng, Xiong Shihui, Wu Zhongxin, Huang Shaoxiong, Chen Lifu, and dozens of others also visited the hospital one after another. Chiang also reported to the committee members at the first general meeting that Wang's treatment was progressing well. Central Hospital officially released the following report on Wang's condition at 11:00 AM: Premier Wang underwent surgery at 4:00 PM on the 1st under local anesthesia to remove several bone fragments and small shrapnel from his left cheek. The wound on his back was cleaned and sutured. He slept comfortably that night. This morning, his temperature was 37.5 degrees Celsius, pulse 82, and respiration 18. Dr. Branch, a physician from Shanghai, arrived in Nanjing early this morning to consult with Director Liu Ruiheng and Chief Physician Shen Kefei. They jointly announced that Premier Wang's injuries were not serious and his condition was good. (Central News Agency dispatch, 2nd)

(Nanjing) Central Hospital Director Liu released a statement at 10:00 AM this morning stating that Premier Wang's health is still satisfactory this morning, with a temperature of 37.5, a pulse of 82, and a respiration rate of 18. The hospital is currently preparing a detailed report on Premier Wang's injuries, which may be released today. (Reuters dispatch, 2nd)

Chaotic Situation After the Incident

Invitation for Miller to Assist in Diagnosis and Treatment

(Nanjing) Premier Wang's condition continued to improve in the afternoon of the 2nd. He consumed chicken broth, orange juice, and other items on schedule, and his spirits were quite comfortable. According to a report released by Central Hospital at 5:00 PM, Premier Wang's wound on his left cheek was bandaged twice. At 4:00 PM, he received an intramuscular injection of 500 units of tetanus antitoxin serum. This injection is a routine procedure for anyone who has suffered a gunshot wound. His temperature was 37.4, pulse 80, and respiration 16. His condition is progressing well. As Wang's injuries gradually healed, Dr. Branch returned to Shanghai in the afternoon to attend to his duties. In order to ensure Premier Wang's speedy recovery, Chu Minyi and others telegraphed Miller, a famous surgeon in the East and director of the Shanghai Sanitarium (currently in Guangzhou), and Niu Huilin to come to Nanjing to assist in diagnosis and treatment. Yu Youren, Ye Chu-cang, and representatives from various agencies, totaling over a hundred people, also visited the hospital in the afternoon. (Central News Agency dispatch, 2nd)

Dr. Noel Flies to Beijing from Baotou

(Guihua) Dr. Noel, who has previously treated Premier Wang's liver disease, came to Suiyuan for hunting last month. After Wang's assassination attempt, Chu Minyi urgently telegraphed Fu Zuoyi on the 1st, instructing him to find Noel and ask him to return to Beijing for treatment. After receiving the telegram, Fu immediately telegraphed the Guyang County government to find him. The county found Noel at noon on the 2nd, and he is scheduled to fly to Beijing from Baotou on the 3rd. (Central News Agency dispatch, 2nd)

Sun Fengming Dies in Hospital

(Nanjing) Sun Fengming, the assassin who attacked Premier Wang, died in the hospital at 3:45 AM on the 2nd after being wounded by the guards. (Special dispatch, 2nd)

(Nanjing) Sun Fengming, the assassin who attacked Premier Wang, was also sent to Central Hospital after being shot by Wang's guards. Because he was shot in vital areas and lost too much blood, he died in the hospital at 3:45 AM on the 2nd. (Central News Agency dispatch, 2nd)

Ministry of Justice Orders Investigation of Assassination Attempt

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Justice believes that the assassination attempt on Premier Wang is a serious case and has ordered the Chief Prosecutor of the Supreme Court Procuratorate to investigate and prosecute the matter. (Central News Agency dispatch, 2nd)

(Nanjing) The military police authorities have instructed all officers under their command to pay attention to apprehending the culprits and bringing them to justice, and to pay special attention to maintaining public order in the city to ensure safety. (Special dispatch, 2nd)

Ten Suspects Released on Bail

(Nanjing) After the assassination attempt on Premier Wang occurred on the 1st, police arrested a total of 18 suspects. Two more were arrested on the 2nd. After two rounds of interrogation, ten have been released on bail, and the remaining one is still being held by the department for investigation. (Special dispatch, 2nd)

Heads of Various Agencies Interrogate the Assassin

(Nanjing) Sun Fengming, the assassin who attacked Premier Wang, was shot twice by Wang's guards on the 1st and sent to Central Hospital for treatment. However, both bullets hit the lungs, precisely in vital areas, and he lost too much blood, so he ultimately succumbed to his injuries. He died at 3:45 AM on the morning of the 2nd. At dawn, the Second Police Bureau transferred the body to the Capital Court. After the Chief Prosecutor Sun Shaokang examined the body, he handed it over to the burial bureau for disposal. He had not yet been buried on the 2nd. After the suspect was sent to the hospital, physicians treated him while senior officials from the Executive Yuan, Military Affairs Commission, Ministry of Foreign Affairs, Ministry of Interior, Military Police Department, Police Department, Supreme Court, and Procuratorate interrogated him rigorously. By noon on the 1st, the suspect was in critical condition. Doctors injected stimulants, and Gu Zhenglun, Chen Zhuo, Tao Luqian, Peng Xuepei, and others jointly interrogated him for a long time. In the end, the suspect repeatedly complained of a headache and refused to speak. There is no doubt that the suspect's attack was a planned conspiracy. After his arrest, six small silver coins, two pieces of American ginseng, three pieces of chewing gum, and one opium pipe were found on his person. The fact that the suspect did not carry a large amount of money indicates that he did not intend to flee far, and the opium pipe suggests that he intended to take advantage of an opportunity to commit suicide. The letter left at the Chenguang News Agency, which was searched by the police department, further proves this. However, according to participating investigators, the motive and background of the assassination are still difficult to speculate. In addition, the twenty suspects arrested on the 1st were taken to the Qingliangshan Police Training Center, where they were jointly interrogated by major officials from the Party, government, military, police, and courts from 8:00 AM to 5:00 PM on the 2nd. Some individuals were found to have little connection to the case, so five were released, seven were released on bail, and eight remain in custody for further questioning. (Central News Agency dispatch, 2nd)

(Nanjing) A reporter visited Central Hospital tonight to inquire about Premier Wang's condition and learned that he is almost out of danger. Surgery was performed this afternoon, and the bullet fragments in his left cheek have been removed, but the bullet in his back has not yet been removed. Sun Fengming, the assassin who attacked Wang, died in Central Hospital at 3:45 AM this morning from his injuries. After receiving the news of Sun's death, the Jiangning District Court immediately conducted an examination and determined that he died from gunshot wounds. The body was handed over to the funeral home for burial. After Sun was arrested yesterday, he was rigorously interrogated by the authorities for several hours. At midnight, Sun became increasingly weak, and doctors injected stimulants to continue the interrogation. According to Sun's confession, the attack on Wang was purely his own initiative and was not directed by anyone else. As for Hu Yunqing, the president of Chenguang News Agency, and He Boguang, the editor-in-chief, they left Beijing at midnight on Thursday. However, some witnesses said that they saw Hu and He on Friday morning, so these two actually left the capital on Friday morning. Hu and He are both natives of Zhenjiang, so the police department has telegraphed the Zhenjiang authorities to conduct a thorough search, but they have not yet been apprehended. After midnight, Sun Fengming complained of severe headaches and refused to answer questions. He died at 3:45 AM. Police searched his pockets and found opium, indicating that he was prepared to commit suicide upon being arrested. It is now known that Hu and He are indeed the main culprits in this case, and the authorities are determined to apprehend them. In addition to the suspect Sun, more than twenty other suspects have been arrested. The police department conducted separate rigorous interrogations from 8:00 AM to 5:00 PM this morning, and as a result, five were released, seven were released on bail, and the remaining eight remain in custody for further questioning. (Reuters dispatch, 2nd)

Sun Fengming, the Assassin Who Died Yesterday Morning

Current Affairs Commentary

The Impact of Speculative Gold Trading 5

— End

As the time approaches for settling long-term deposit accounts at the end of the year, there is concern that gold prices have suddenly experienced an unusual surge. In the past half-month, foreign exchange rates have risen sharply, commodity prices have soared, and speculation has led to extreme price fluctuations. It is natural that society is shocked and people are uneasy. Those who are not familiar with the concept of inflation believe that it is simply due to the increased issuance of paper money. As a result, those with cash are trying to hide it, and those with assets believe that it is better to hoard goods for speculation than to hold currency and suffer losses. The demand for gold and foreign exchange bills has further increased, and silver has unexpectedly concentrated in foreign banks, with the premium reaching as high as seventy cents, remaining unchanged for four days. Chinese entities have been selling silver in the London market continuously for eighteen days without stopping. It is not surprising that capital is moving towards safe havens. However, China is suffering from a shortage of silver. Last winter, there was a move to levy a balancing tax. Although silver imports exceeded seven million in the third quarter of this year, gold exports exceeded thirteen million, resulting in a net outflow.

Since gold prices are settled in Customs Gold Units, it is generally understood that it is not easy for foreign businesses to convert currency freely. However, gold prices have continued to rise daily recently. The authorities have intervened to maintain stability, but with little effect. As a result, rumors that the Gold Exchange Standard will be implemented and Customs Gold Unit notes will be issued have become increasingly prevalent. It is clear that such talk seems plausible but is not actually true. Currency reform has its own steps and preparations and cannot be achieved instantaneously. However, the general public believes that without a strong correction, it is best to just listen and see what happens. The most worrying aspect is that the continuous rise in gold prices has made everyone wary of legitimate transactions. For example, silk and other commodities have seen a decrease in recent transactions due to this reason. If it is once known that the rumors are false, the reaction will be unstoppable. Both of these losses are due to speculators.

For the sake of the overall situation, we feel compelled to speak out on the following points: (1) In today's environment of exhausted commercial finance, the chaotic situation of speculation cannot last long. Sitting idly by without taking remedial action will only create a more serious situation and accelerate the flight of capital. Therefore, the authorities should make a clearer and more responsible statement to reassure the public. (2) Given the complexity of China's political and economic situation and the distorted structure of the market, any reform should avoid actions that are counterproductive. However, past observations reveal that opportunities have often been created for foreigners, which is regrettable. (3) The shift of credit from domestic to foreign entities has been a long-standing issue. The early use of foreign currency notes and the recent willingness to exchange large amounts of cash for a piece of paper from a foreign bank show that the Chinese people are not without the concept of fiduciary money. If it can be used well, who knows if it cannot be successful? Therefore, how to establish a credible system, shift the psychological dependence on foreign entities, and gain the trust of the people are critical issues to address today. (4) Global finance is still difficult to stabilize, and currency adjustments are extremely difficult. Although news from the United States suggests that the Chinese currency will be stabilized at 2.5 Customs Gold Units and 26.8 US cents, given China's large trade deficit, meager income from sources other than trade, and various other obstacles, this seems unlikely. (5) At this time of great difficulty and pressing external threats, reform is more difficult than usual. Conspiracies and sabotage are rampant. Therefore, how to preserve a line of survival for our national economy depends on having an independent spirit and the will to survive on our own.

A follow-up telegram of sympathy stated that after slightly taking some milk this morning, President Wang immediately asked for the newspaper, but only briefly looked at the headlines. Then, Madame Wang read three news items on his behalf. This morning, Vice Minister of Interior Tao Lujian, Police Commissioner Chen Zhuo, Commander of the Gendarmerie Gu Zhenglun, Director of the Executive Yuan's Political Affairs Department Peng Xuepei, Vice Minister of Transportation Zhang Daofan, and Vice Minister of Industry Gu Zhenggang jointly opened a court to interrogate the prisoners arrested yesterday. The content was kept strictly confidential. (Reuters, 2nd)

(Nanjing) After Chairman Lin received a telegram of sympathy and concern from the Southwest Political Committee, he replied on the 2nd. The content was roughly the same as the telegram sent by Chu Minyi on the 1st regarding the assassination attempt on President Wang. (Central News Agency, 2nd)

(Hankou) After the news of the attack on President Wang by an assailant and his injuries reached Hankou on the 1st, consuls from various countries and overseas Chinese flocked to the office of the Special Commissioner of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs for Hunan and Hubei to express their condolences. Commissioner Xiao Encheng personally received them and expressed his gratitude. Xiao had already telegraphed Wang to report the situation yesterday. (Central News Agency, 2nd)

(Changsha) After the news of the assassination attempt on President Wang reached Hunan, He Jian telegraphed his condolences to the capital on the night of the 1st. (Central News Agency, 2nd)

(Anqing) When the news of the assassination attempt on President Wang was received, all parties were greatly shocked. The provincial party headquarters and the provincial government have both sent telegrams of condolence. (Central News Agency, 2nd)

(Nanchang) All sectors of Gan Province were extremely concerned about Wang's condition upon hearing the news of the assassination attempt. The provincial government specially telegraphed its condolences to the capital on the 2nd. (Central News Agency, 2nd)

British Newspapers Express Great Concern

(London) This morning, all newspapers paid close attention to the assassination attempt on Chinese President Wang. The diplomatic correspondent of the Morning Post stated that Londoners considered this assassination to be a very significant event. The Daily Telegraph reported that the assassination attempt on President Wang was a warning about the various difficulties faced by Nanjing. Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, with the assistance of President Wang and others, had made great progress in the past four years towards the restoration of order and unity in China. Although the activities of the Communist Party had spread to some extent this summer, they were still limited to smaller areas. As for the economy, there had been significant progress. The Times stated that this case was a pre-planned riot. President Wang was a sincere and patriotic politician who had devoted himself to the revolution and was now a constructive member of the Nanjing government. We deeply hope that the fears of future disputes arising from his health will not be proven by facts. (Reuters, 1st)

Japanese Newspapers Add Color and Exaggeration

(Nanjing) After President Wang was injured by an assailant on the morning of the 1st, Japanese newspapers exaggerated in many ways, claiming that other important figures were also injured, or speculating on the background of the assassination. The Information Division of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs specially sent Section Chief Shao to visit the Japanese Embassy and requested their attention, and to convey to the Japanese newspaper offices that they should act cautiously to avoid being accused of inciting conflict. It is reported that the Japanese Embassy has expressed its intention to comply. Shao also warned the Japanese reporters stationed in Nanjing that they must have reliable evidence when publishing news in the future and must not fabricate information based on conjecture. (Central News Agency, 2nd)

Fuzhou Agreed on Measures to Restrict the Outflow of Gold and Silver 6

(Fuzhou) Gold and silver prices here are rising, and there is an apparent shortage of silver dollars. Specific measures have been decided. In the future, restrictions will be placed on withdrawals of cash from banks, and the use of the funds will be investigated and submitted to the Public Security Bureau for verification. (Special Dispatch, 21st)

Setting up a company in Shanghai will have to wait until the Tianjin company is established and effectively operating. (Special Dispatch, 2nd)

Japanese Troops Stationed in Beiping-Tianjin-Yuguan Preparing for Autumn Maneuvers, Starting Tomorrow 10

(Beiping) The Japanese troops stationed in Beiping, Tianjin, and Yuguan have decided to hold large-scale autumn maneuvers along the Beijing-Ningbo Railway from the 4th to the 7th. The Beijing-Ningbo Railway Bureau has prepared nine trains to transport officers, soldiers, and baggage in stages from various stations. The Japanese troops stationed in Beiping are scheduled to depart on the morning of the 4th to participate in the exercises and return to Beiping on the evening of the 7th. (Special Dispatch, 2nd)

(Tianjin) The Japanese army's autumn military exercises in North China have been prepared and will begin at 9 a.m. on the 4th for three days, along the Beiping-Tianjin section of the Beijing-Ningbo Railway, until noon on the 7th. On the 4th, an encounter battle will be held in Langfang, along with camping; on the 5th, field exercises will be held in the Weishanzhuang Huangcun area, along with camping; and on the 6th, attack and defense exercises will be held near Fengtai, along with camping. The participating troops include 300 infantry from Beiping, commanded by Captain Hasegawa; 300 infantry from Tianjin, 200 field and mountain artillery, commanded by Captain Kayashima; and cavalry and supply troops from Tanggu will also join as a separate detachment. Armored vehicles and tanks from Beiping and Tianjin will all be deployed. (Special Dispatch, 2nd)

Oii Arrives in Tianjin to Negotiate Telecommunications Between Guannei and Guanwai 11

(Tianjin) Japanese Vice Minister of Communications Oii came to Tianjin, visited the Tianjin Telegraph Bureau, and met with Director Wang Ruoxi to discuss matters related to communications between Guannei (inside the customs) and Guanwai (outside the customs). On the 2nd, Oii visited Gu Zhen, director of the Tianjin Telephone Bureau, to discuss long-distance telephone exchanges and communications between Guannei and Guanwai. Oii is scheduled to go to Shenyang on the 3rd. Regarding the issue of Japanese telegrams between Guannei and Guanwai, according to the person in charge of the Tianjin Telegraph Bureau, it is limited to wired telegraph transmissions between Tianjin and Shenyang. The Tianjin General Bureau is the only telegraph bureau in Guannei, and Shenyang is the telegraph bureau in Guanwai. When Japanese people in the Kwantung Leased Territory and the South Manchuria Railway Zone in Jilin, Changchun, Harbin, and Qiqihar send Japanese telegrams, they are forwarded by the Shenyang Wired Telegraph Bureau. This does not mean that all wireless telegraphs can be sent and received. However, Chinese telegrams can be sent and received by wireless telegraphs, regardless of the Tianjin-Shenyang line. (Special Dispatch, 2nd)

(Tianjin) The telegraph bureau established by the Japanese in Shanhaiguan is a "helping telegraph bureau" dedicated to handling the transfer of Japanese telegrams between Guannei and Guanwai. Due to the excessive length and weak power of the Tianjin-Shenyang line, in order to speed up transmission, the Tianjin Bureau sends telegrams to the Yuguan Telegraph Bureau, which then forwards them to the Japanese "helping telegraph bureau" before forwarding them to the Shenyang Bureau. The procedure for incoming telegrams is the same. Although the Beiping Telegraph Bureau is actively preparing, the exact date for receiving and sending Japanese telegrams has not yet been determined. (Special Dispatch, 2nd)

Descendants of the Zhu Family Sell Ancient Cypress Trees in the Ming Tombs in Changping Without Authorization 12

(Beiping) The ancient cypress trees in the Ming Tombs in Changping County, originally under the custody of descendants of the Zhu family, were suddenly sold to the Japanese without authorization. About two hundred of these ancient cypress trees, of which over sixty have been cut down, were discovered by the county government. Since the matter concerns antiquities, they should be protected. In addition to ordering a halt to the cutting, the case has been reported to the authorities for investigation. Shang Zhen ordered the Ji-Mi District Commissioner's Office to handle the matter yesterday. It is reported that negotiations have been held with the Japanese side. (Special Dispatch, 2nd)

Northwest Headquarters Officially Established, Important Officials Announced 13

(Xi'an) The Northwest Bandit Suppression Headquarters was officially established on the 1st, and the officials have been selected and announced. They include: Chief of Staff Qian Dajun, Secretary-General Wu Jiaxiang, Director of the Office Mi Chunlin, Deputy Director Wang Yuke, Director of the First Division Xu Fang, Deputy Director Wang Zhongsheng, Director of the Second Division Min Xiangfan, Deputy Director Gao Songshan, Director of the Third Division Ma Zhaoqi, Deputy Director Wang Baozhong, Director of the Fourth Division Zhou Congzheng, Deputy Director Wang Fuzhou, Director of the Military Law Office Zhao Hongzhu, Director of the Transportation Office Jiang Bin, and several other section chiefs and lower-level staff. They began working immediately. (Central News Agency, 2nd)

(Xi'an) The Northwest Bandit Suppression Headquarters was officially established on the 1st. All officers and soldiers held a flag-raising ceremony at 9 a.m., and all offices began formal operations. (Central News Agency, 1st)

Smuggling Organizations Discovered in Xiamen 14

(Xiamen) Large-scale land and sea smuggling organizations have been discovered here. They specialize in transporting silver, cloth, medicinal materials, seafood, sugar, oil, matches, and other subsidiary goods from Taiwan, distributing them to various places in Zhangzhou, Quanzhou, and Xiamen. The organization is tightly knit, with some kind of background as a protective amulet, and some civil servants are participating. They have made profits of over 400,000 yuan in four months. The silver transported here is sold after being smuggled through Hong Kong. (Special Dispatch, 2nd)

National Government Announces Disaster Relief Bond Regulations, Implementation Measures for Disaster Relief Reserve Fund Also Announced 15

(Nanjing) The National Government issued an order on the 1st, announcing the Regulations on Public Bonds for Water Disaster Relief and Work Relief in the 24th Year of the Republic of China. This order. (Central News Agency, 2nd)

(Nanjing) The National Government issued a decree on the 2nd, announcing the Provisional Measures for the Implementation of the Disaster Relief Reserve Fund. The full text contains ten articles and will be implemented immediately. (Central News Agency, 2nd)

Water Level Continues to Rise in Peixian 16

(Xuzhou) A telephone call from Peixian on the 2nd stated that Peixian city is surrounded by floods, and the water level continues to rise, more than four feet above the city. Many earthen embankments have collapsed, and with continuous wind and rain in recent days, the northwestern and southwestern city embankments have repeatedly collapsed, causing extreme danger. The county government and various agencies and schools have all suspended operations and are mobilizing to prevent floods and protect the city. (Central News Agency, 2nd)

Xinpu Xinkai River Completed, Salt River Discharges Smoothly 17

(Xuzhou) According to a Hai message, the Xinpu Xinkai River was completed yesterday, and the Salt River discharges smoothly. The water level has fallen to its original state, and the water level in each river has fallen, and the submerged land has gradually emerged. (Special Dispatch, 2nd)

(Xuzhou) All sectors of Shuyang are concerned that the downstream of each river in Shuyang enters the Salt River in Guanyun, and that there are many dams built to block the river on the east bank of the Salt River, with reeds covering the beaches, blocking the water flow. They have jointly telegraphed the Economic Commission, the Jiangsu Provincial Government, the Huai River Diversion Office, and the Donghai Special Office, requesting that the Guanyun County Magistrate be ordered to quickly demolish all dams east of the Salt River and clear the Wutu River Liezikou to facilitate discharge. (Special Dispatch, 2nd)

(Xuzhou) In order to avoid flooding of the Salt River, Guanyun plans to dredge the river channel, including dredging the Cenchi River, dredging the new and old Shaoxiang Rivers, and dredging the Xin Salt River and the Post-Disaster River, requiring 190,000 yuan. County Magistrate Xu Xieqi recently went to the province to negotiate, and the Ministry of Finance ordered the Audit Office to allocate 60,000 yuan, and the Provincial Government allocated 20,000 yuan, planning to use work as a substitute for disaster relief, and will start construction soon. It is investigated that the Yellow River's seawater irrigation is due to excessive water volume. The salt ponds north of the east corner mountain of Guanyun were all washed away. It is reported that after a flush of fresh water, it will take more than a year before salt can be re-exposed, and the salt industry has suffered a great loss. (Special Dispatch, 2nd)

Ministry of Finance Does Not Allow Changes to Stamp Tax Rate on Insurance Policies 18

(Nanjing) The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce and the Insurance Association jointly submitted a request to the Ministry of Finance, stating that the stamp tax rate on insurance policies stipulated in the Stamp Tax Law was too heavy, requesting that it still be approved to apply the revised stamping method as approved in the 18th year of the Republic of China to show sympathy. The Ministry of Finance replied yesterday that the matter concerned changes to the law, and it was not appropriate to approve it. (Special Dispatch, 2nd)

(Nanjing) The second group of ten judges transferred from the High Courts of various provinces to Beijing by the Supreme Court to clear backlog cases have reported and started working on the 1st. (Central News Agency, 2nd)

League of Nations to Impose Economic Sanctions Starting on the 18th of This Month 21

Representatives of Fifty Nations Unanimously Agree, Anglo-Italian Negotiations Fail Once Again, French Foreign Minister Pursuing a Different Path

(Geneva) The Committee of Eighteen of the League of Nations decided today to recommend to the General Committee that economic sanctions be imposed on Italy, effective November 18th. (National News Agency, 2nd)

(Geneva) The fifty nations in the Sanctions Committee unanimously agreed on that date, but Chile made certain reservations. French Prime Minister Laval gave a short speech, reiterating his belief that the League of Nations could resolve the Italian-Ethiopian dispute and that he had begun talks with Italy based on the Franco-Italian friendship treaty. He assured the committee that France would not act outside the League of Nations. (Reuters, 2nd)

(Geneva) British Foreign Secretary Hoare held a three-quarter-hour conversation with Italian representative Aloisi this morning. It is reported that Hoare detailed Britain's position and clearly stated that while Britain was eager to see a peaceful resolution, a resolution unfavorable to the Ethiopian Emperor or in conflict with the League of Nations Covenant was out of the question. It is now understood that no new basis for negotiation exists, but the search will continue. At the same time, both sides are eager to dispel the mistaken impression that there are any special disputes between Britain and Italy. This impression was caused by Italian anti-British propaganda and the large number of Italian troops stationed in Libya. If this impression can be removed and the tense atmosphere eased, it would be welcomed by both countries. (Reuters, 2nd)

(Geneva) It was learned here today that Italy has rejected the recent draft peace plan proposed by Britain and France. Italian chief delegate to the League of Nations, Sir Aloisi, made it clear during his meetings with Laval and Hoare that the East African war would continue. Sir Aloisi told Italian journalists today that if the proposals put forward by Laval this afternoon were all there was, there would be no hope for peace. Hoare and Aloisi, who were originally scheduled to talk again tomorrow, have been canceled today. The talk that reconciliation is hopeless has thus become more forceful. The League of Nations learned that Germany may follow the United States in banning the transportation of armaments and munitions to belligerent countries. (National Telegram, 1st)

(Geneva) Hoare and Laval informed each other of the impressions gained from their meetings with Italian representative Aloisi during lunch today and agreed on the speeches they would make in the Sanctions Committee this afternoon. It was rumored that the representatives of Britain, France, and Belgium had exchanged views on the Locarno Pact in Geneva, but this was not the case. Belgian Prime Minister Kollen claimed that he intended to request that the Sanctions Committee pass a resolution authorizing Britain and France to conduct negotiations on behalf of the League of Nations to peacefully resolve the Italian-Ethiopian dispute. (Havas, 2nd)

Obstacles to Sanctions 22

(Geneva) The eighteen-nation committee's discussion on implementing sanctions against Italy should not hinder the issue of Italy's 32,950,000,000 yuan in bad debts owed to member states, resulting in a deadlock. During today's meeting, representatives from Romania, Yugoslavia, and Chile successively stated that Italy pays with goods, so if they refuse to accept Italian goods, they will sacrifice their debts. A small committee will now be organized to study this issue. (1st National Telegraph)

(Geneva) Representatives from France, Romania, Yugoslavia, Spain, and Greece held a small committee meeting to discuss settling accounts with Italy. Many countries, especially Romania, are owed large sums of money by Italy, making their situation particularly difficult. This fact is an obstacle to the implementation of sanctions against Italy. The meeting lasted five hours, and a solution was finally agreed upon at 1:00 AM, stipulating that a date should be set for stopping the purchase of Italian goods. As for unsettled debts, they will be specifically considered by the small committee dealing with mutual aid issues. (2nd Reuters)

(Geneva) The implementation of economic sanctions against Italy was discussed here today, with attention paid to the date of implementation and the difficulties regarding settling contracts. However, a solution to the contract settlement issue has not yet been agreed upon. A small committee of representatives from Britain, France, Romania, Yugoslavia, Spain, and Greece will meet tonight to discuss and decide on this matter. Italian General Representative Aloisi visited French Prime Minister Laval tonight. Although no statement was issued, it is said that general issues were discussed, but no solutions were proposed. Aloisi will meet with British Foreign Secretary Hoare tomorrow. Eden is currently packing and plans to return to London on Saturday evening. (1st Reuters)

(Geneva) During today's meeting of the eighteen-nation committee, the Canadian representative suddenly proposed a ban on the transportation of oil, oil products, coal, and iron to Italy and Italian territories. Representatives from Britain, France, and South Africa all strongly supported this proposal. This move would hinder Italy's colonial war more severely than attacks by the Abyssinian army on its lines of communication, as Italy does not produce the coal needed for transport ships, nor does it produce the gasoline needed for tanks and airplanes. The committee decided to transfer this proposal to the technical committee, but the attitude of non-member states is the main factor in this complex issue, so no decision will be made before mid-December. (2nd Reuters)

Melbourne The Australian Prime Minister, Lyons, has now stated that the Deputy Chairman of the Executive Council, Hughes, formerly the Australian Prime Minister during the European War, had differing opinions with the authorities regarding sanctions against Italy, so the Prime Minister has requested his withdrawal from the cabinet. (2nd Reuters)

Italian Military Transport Vehicles on the Northern Front, Advancing Like a Long Snake 23

Ciano Also Leads the Air Force to Reconnoiter Abyssinian Capital Denies 3,500 Casualties

Asmara Transport vehicles are today advancing to the front lines like a long snake. The tense atmosphere indicates that the Italian army on the northern front is about to launch an offensive. Magal has not yet fallen, but it shows signs of wavering at any moment. Prime Minister Mussolini's son-in-law, Ciano, led the air force on a mission today. (1st National Telegraph)

(Rome) Today, a telegram was received here from General De Bono, Commander-in-Chief of the Italian Army in East Africa, stating that after the Italian army's renewed activity in the north, they are currently conducting extensive reconnaissance operations in the area between Haranate and Chiralte. A large number of people in Tigre province have requested permission to serve in the Italian army, so a volunteer force has been formed to guard the borders. General Badoglio, Chief of Staff of the Italian Army, has returned today from inspecting the East African war zone. (2nd Reuters)

Abyssinian Capital The Abyssinian government officially denies the claim that Magal has been captured by the Italian army. (2nd Reuters)

Abyssinian Capital The authorities here deny the claim that 3,500 Abyssinian soldiers were killed or wounded in the fierce battle at Worgaden. This news was transmitted to a Paris newspaper by a correspondent stationed here. It is said that the Abyssinian army fought fiercely around Walwal in an attempt to capture the town, but failed, and the Abyssinian commander, Tai Gashi, was killed in this battle. (2nd Reuters)

Asmara General De Bono, Commander-in-Chief of the Italian Army on the Northern Front, today expressed his determination to continue the offensive against Abyssinia. De Bono told the Associated Press reporter that "We are actively carrying out a plan to spread culture in savage areas, which is no different from what other countries have done in the past." Regarding the League of Nations' implementation of economic sanctions, De Bono said, "We value these sanctions, but we also wish to realize our desires. Italy has now exhausted all peaceful means to complete its colonial plan, but it can also cope with any resistance." (1st National News Agency)

Abyssinian Capital Governor Dengdu of Sidamo Province reported today that another Italian bomber was shot down. It was previously reported that an Italian plane was shot down five days ago. (5th National Telegraph)

(Rome) The authorities here announced today that a total of 193 officers and soldiers have died since January 1 of this year due to battle or other causes. The majority of these deaths are related to the East African war, but not all were caused by combat. In addition to officers and soldiers, 198 workers have also died. (1st National Telegraph)

Italian Party and Government to Hold Supreme Meeting 10,000 More Party Soldiers to Ship to East Africa 24

(Rome) The Supreme Council of the Fascist Party is scheduled to meet at 10:00 PM on November 16 at the Venice Palace. The cabinet is scheduled to meet on November 30. (1st Havas)

Naples The "January 3rd Division" and the "February 1st Division" of the Blackshirts, totaling about 10,000 people, are scheduled to sail to East Africa on Sunday. A portion of them, including 68 officers and 600 soldiers, have already sailed to the port of Massawa today on the "Aventino." Fifteen more officers and 544 soldiers will depart tonight. (1st Havas)

(Rome) The government has recently taken strict measures to prevent speculation in daily food items. A coffee importer in the port of Genoa has been charged with charging excessive prices, and the authorities have revoked the merchant's Fascist Party membership card as punishment. In the capital, two merchants, one selling soap at a price exceeding the official price, and the other hoarding goods with the intention of making exorbitant profits, have been arrested and sent to the judicial authorities for interrogation. (1st Havas)

(Rome) The Italian government has recently banned Eritrean merchants from transporting and exporting cattle and sheep hides produced within the territory, and stipulated that these hides must be used entirely for leather production to meet the needs of the front lines. In addition, the National Railway Administration, in order to comply with the government's order to save consumption, has decided to cancel 46 train services nationwide from November 6, including several express trains. (2nd Havas)

Italy Again Demonstrates Against Britain 25

(Rome) There were renewed anti-British demonstrations here today. The glass window of a store displaying British materials, marked with the words "British Cloth," was destroyed by about 150 people. Stores with British goods are now afraid to display them or deny that they are British goods. Biscuits that are clearly made in Britain have their packaging covered with other paper. Importers are complaining because they can hardly withdraw British goods from customs. Students are posting notices in the streets, urging the public to only buy domestic goods. A British hotel, one of the oldest in Rome, has covered its name in front of the hotel with the Italian flag. British tea houses are also taking similar precautions. (1st Reuters)

(Rome) Italian students held an anti-British demonstration in Rome today, attacking pro-British shops, hotels, and tea rooms. The demonstrators also smashed windows and signs, warning shop owners not to use foreign store names. For example, the Eden Hotel was among those warned. Another group of students ordered the manager of the British Hotel to cover the words "British" on the signboard with the Fascist Party flag. One hundred guards in front of the British Embassy are on high alert at night. (1st National News Agency)

(Rome) The Italian newspapers today continue to disregard Britain's warning that the British fleet will remain in the Mediterranean until anti-British propaganda ends. Italian Daily News editor Gaeta wrote an article today criticizing Britain, accusing it of intending to keep Abyssinia for future British expansion. Gaeta directly called British Prime Minister Baldwin and other British leaders liars, and advised Italians not to recognize Britain's motives as worship of the League of Nations covenant, but to see them as imperialist conspiracies. (1st National News Agency)

Japanese Communications Minister Mochizuki Encourages the Organization of a Large News Agency Invites Representatives of the National Press to Discuss the Matter in View of the Immediate Need Due to the International Situation 26

(Tokyo) Major news agencies across Japan and the Japan Broadcasting Corporation are attempting to establish a world-class international news agency in Japan. They have applied to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and the Ministry of Communications for permission to establish a new corporate entity, the Allied News Agency. However, at that time, due to Minister of Communications Tokonami's inability to carry out the matter, the work of establishing a new news agency was resumed after Mochizuki took office as Minister of Communications. Recently, Minister of Communications Mochizuki, in view of the international situation, confirmed that establishing a powerful news agency is an urgent task at present. On the morning of the 2nd, at 11:00 AM, he invited representatives of major news agencies and news agencies nationwide to the Minister of Communications' official residence to explain the government's beliefs and request the cooperation of the representatives. Minister of Communications Mochizuki made the following points: "There is no need to elaborate on the reasons why it is necessary to strengthen the communications industry today. Former Minister of Communications Tokonami and Foreign Minister Hirota expressed this to you in May. Recently, a conflict has occurred between Italy and Abyssinia, and major news agencies around the world are very active. In view of the international situation, it is extremely important from a national policy perspective to unify the communications industry as soon as possible and realize its strengthening. This time, the national press and broadcasting associations are cooperating to organize a public interest corporation to establish a large news agency under the fairest conditions, which is a project that suits the current era. The government has now decided to approve its establishment. I hope that the national news and communications agencies will cooperate to make its plan a success." After Minister of Communications Mochizuki finished speaking, the Minister of Communications, Vice Ministers Aomoto and Ohashi, Participating Official Hirano, Director of the Telecommunications Bureau Shindo, and Vice Minister of Foreign Affairs Shigemitsu, Director of the Information Department Amau, and others exchanged various opinions with the news representatives. The meeting adjourned at 2:00 PM. The official order approving the establishment of the Allied News Agency is expected to be issued in two or three days. (2nd Rengo)

Debuchi Suggests to Hirota that Japanese-Australian Trade Principles Should First Establish Close Relations 27

(Tokyo) Ambassador Debuchi, who was dispatched to Australia, met with Foreign Minister Hirota at 10:00 AM on the morning of the 2nd. After reporting on his mission, he made the following important suggestions regarding trade with Australia: (1) Australia and New Zealand have very good feelings towards Japan, and are enthusiastic about maintaining friendly relations with Japan. (2) If Japan wants to develop trade in the South Pacific, it should first establish close relations with these countries. It is essential to obtain their assistance through economic principles. (2nd Rengo)

British Bank Establishes Committee to Protect the Interests of Chinese Bondholders Result of Ross's Visit to China 28

(London) According to a statement released yesterday, the Governor of the Bank of England has established a committee to find ways to protect the interests of British holders of Chinese railway bonds and other bonds. This move is the result of British government economic advisor Sir Arthur Salter's visit to China. The committee consists of five members, chaired by Lord Alness. Today, The Times published an editorial stating that this move will surely be welcomed by many people in Britain who hold Chinese securities, some of whom are uneasy due to the large drop in Shanghai exchange rates. There have recently been suggestions as to whether action should be taken to protect their position. Financial News has learned that the organization of this committee is due to the fact that since President Roosevelt implemented his silver policy, one wave has followed another, and there has been no peace. The Bank of England's actions have been welcomed by all sectors in London. It should be stated that the Chinese bond market has not yet been shaken by the exchange rate market. The Chinese Committee will not be concerned with any possibilities regarding commercial loans, and will focus solely on protecting the position of bonds. The committee represents the interests of various large foreign bond investments. (2nd Reuters)

Current State of Sino-U.S. Trade 29

(Washington) The Department of Commerce announced today that imports of Chinese goods in September were less than in August, but more than in the same period last year. Imports in September of this year were worth a total of 4,317,522, a decrease of 15% compared to August, but an increase of 24% compared to September of last year. Conversely, the goods exported to China were more than in August, but less than in September of last year. Exports in September of this year were worth a total of 2,461,518 yuan, compared to 1,740,051 yuan in September of last year. Imports of Chinese goods in the first nine months of this year were worth approximately 46,008,272 yuan, compared to 34,681,522 yuan in the same period a year ago. Exports were worth a total of 29,132,267 yuan, compared to 45,809,269 yuan in the first nine months of 1934. (1st National Telegraph)

United States Suspends Trade Agreement Negotiations with Italy 30

(Washington) The State Department has suspended negotiations between the United States and Italy on concluding a trade agreement, as this agreement is incompatible with President Roosevelt's position against trade with warring countries. (1st Reuters)

(Washington) Italian Ambassador to the United States Rosso visited Secretary of State Hull today, stating that negotiations on a trade agreement between Italy and the United States began before the outbreak of the Italian-Abyssinian conflict, and asked for clarification as to whether President Roosevelt's neutrality declaration would have an impact on these negotiations. The results of the conversation are unknown, but it is generally believed that the U.S. government will seek a win-win solution, maintaining the neutrality declaration on the one hand and continuing the State Department's efforts to conclude reciprocal trade agreements on the other. In addition, Under Secretary of State Phillips declared to the press that the Italian-U.S. trade agreement is still under study, but there are many difficulties. (1st Havas)

Dutch Economy Worsens 31

The Hague The government issued a statement today saying that the economic situation in the Netherlands is deteriorating daily. The cabinet still believes that lowering the value of the currency will not help. The budget for 1936 will be limited to a shortfall of 109,000,000 guilders. (1st Reuters)

Soviet Economic Construction 32

(Moscow) As the 18th anniversary of the October Revolution approaches, Soviet newspapers are detailing the construction of the national economy, with the most attention paid to the metallurgical and machine manufacturing industries. The Soviet Union's pig iron production has ranked first in Europe for more than three years. The average daily production of this item in September of this year was approximately 35,000 tons, double that of 1912. The nickel steel industry ranks second in Europe, after Germany. Its average daily production in September of this year was 35,160 tons, more than double that of 1932. The Soviet Union's machine production has ranked first in Europe since 1931. Three years ago, the Soviet Union's automobile production ranked 24th in the world. Today, it has surpassed Italy, Belgium, Sweden, Austria, Czechoslovakia, and other countries, and has jumped to fifth place in the world. (1st TASS)

Alma-Ata The Karaganda-Balkhash railway has laid 443 kilometers of track and is nearing completion. (1st TASS)

Khabarovsk The final workshop of the newly established oil refinery here has been completed. The plant will henceforth supply the area with sufficient kerosene products. Previously, these products had to be imported from central Soviet Union. (1st TASS)

Nagaevo The Kolyma region in northeastern Soviet Union is developing rapidly. The city of Magadan, established only a few years ago, now has a radio station, automobile repair shop, automobile company warehouse, brick kiln, tannery, shipyard, wharf, club, sports field, and cultural recreation park. Nagaevo is now the most well-equipped port on the Sea of Okhotsk. There are many ships on the Kolyma River. The area now has 29 hospitals and 150 medical stations. The number of students in schools has quadrupled in recent years. Local people are now being trained to become agricultural experts and teachers. The area is rich in resources, and its future development is limitless. (1st TASS)

Major Reshuffle of Japanese Army Personnel Imminent 33

(Tokyo) The Army Ministry's Personnel Bureau is currently considering the plan to reshuffle personnel in December. Army Minister Kawashima is scheduled to take this draft plan to Kyoto on the 5th to attend army exercises. He will take the opportunity to meet with Vice Chief of Staff Prince Kan'in-no-miya to request his opinion, and after consulting with Director General of Education Watanabe, he will hold a three-chiefs meeting to formally decide. The scope of this reshuffle is quite broad. Army commanders, division commanders, vice chiefs of staff, headquarters chiefs of the Director General of Education, aviation headquarters, and other central figures will also be reshuffled. It is reported that the reshuffle of important figures will be as follows: Commander of the Korean Army Ueda will be transferred to the position of military councillor. Commander of the Konoe Division Asaka and Commander of the 4th Division Kurahashi, both members of the imperial family, will be promoted to military councillors. Chief of Staff Sugiyama will be appointed as army commander, and Commander of the 1st Division Yanagawa and Commander of the 10th Division Tatekawa are hoping to succeed as chief of staff. International Commercial Telegram 34

—October 2nd Reuters Special Commercial Report—

Gold and Silver

London Gold Price Today is 141 shillings 5 and a half pence, down one and a half pence.

London Silver Market Today's spot price is unchanged, still 29 and three-one-two-five pence. Futures fell one-two-five to 28 and eight-seven-five pence. The United States bought, and China sold.

Exchange Rates

British-American The London foreign exchange market was stable this morning. The opening exchange rate for British-American was 4 yuan 9 jiao 1 fen 625, the same as the closing price for American-British yesterday. An hour later, it rose by 1875 to 4 yuan 9 jiao 1 fen 8125. At closing, it continued to rise by 125, reaching 4 yuan 9 jiao 1 fen 9375, 3125 higher than the opening price.

British-French The opening price was 74 francs 59, 3 pounds higher than yesterday's closing price. Within the first hour, it rose another 3 pounds to 74 francs 62. At noon, it rose another pound to 74 francs 63, after which there were no further changes.

Cotton and Wheat

New York Cotton The cotton market was quiet today. The opening price rose slightly, but gradually fell later. It is said that yarn factories are using quite a lot. The cotton cloth market is sluggish, and prices are relatively loose. The base price of raw cotton remains very strong.

Chicago Wheat The opening prices for wheat and miscellaneous grains both rose slightly today, but due to stagnant trading, prices all fell loosely. The situation in Canada is making the wheat market unstable. Merchants are unwilling to trade much until the policy is announced.

Liverpool Wheat Quiet today. At 1:00 PM, the price for December was 6 shillings and 2 pence, the same as yesterday's closing price.

Liverpool Cotton Stable today. At 1:00 PM, the price for January was 6.12, up one pound.

Rubber

London The market was quiet today. At noon, the trading price for January-March was 6 pence 4375, the same as yesterday's closing price.

New York The market continued to weaken. The opening price plummeted. Later, there was profit-taking, and prices continued to fall.

Securities

New York The market continued to be firm. The opening price was stable. Before noon, it trended upwards. Metal stocks were quite firm. Automobile stocks were bought. The Dow Jones 30 Industrial Average opened at 141.50, up 19 pounds. The New York Stock Market prices are listed below:

Economic Discussions 50

— Edited by Tang Qingzeng

Preface

The economic system is the center of society, and economic power is the driving force for promoting social progress. Today's world is almost entirely dominated by economic forces. If this problem cannot be solved, all complex and chaotic problems will have no way to start. Our country's current economic ills, such as the backwardness of industrial production, the collapse of agriculture, and the low purchasing power of the people, have become deeply ingrained, and dangerous signs have been fully exposed. As for Western countries, the deepness of the panic and tariff wars are not easy to handle and are closely related to our country.

China is currently in need of economic construction, so economic principles and facts are indispensable knowledge for the people of the country. The mission of this column is to use the power of words to promote economic knowledge and analyze reality, in order to arouse readers' interest in and accurate understanding of economic matters. This is one wish of this column.

The scope of this column generally includes: (1) explanation of various basic economic concepts, (2) explanation of modern economic organizations, (3) exploration of special economic issues, (4) investigation of economic conditions in various regions. The content and writing should be simple and accurate, and the materials should be new and complete.

We hope that enthusiastic readers will give this column fair criticism and guidance.

Investment by Wu Depei

In recent years, the rapid tide of the world economic panic has poured into our country. Industry and commerce have declined, the number of unemployed has increased sharply, the market has been sluggish, and floating capital has accumulated and stagnated. It is deposited in banks, and because the bank credit foundation fluctuates, it is not easy to lend money. Individuals and commercial organizations with accumulated cash have also shown an excess phenomenon, and they have to study investment together in order to obtain the benefits they deserve. Recently, due to the European and Asian situation and currency system rumors, public debt prices in this city have soared, and buyer appetite has been strong. This is a major turning point in the investment world.

(1) Characteristics of Investment

Investors put surplus funds into production channels (The Productive Employment of Capital) in order to obtain appropriate interest and enable the original principal to produce "reproduction" effects. The target of investment must be active production and in line with economic principles. Otherwise, investing useful funds in unproductive businesses is abandoning capital rather than investing.

Therefore, the special requirement of investment is the safety of the principal first. Prudent investors must first seek to protect their capital properly. They must not be obsessed with profit and haggle over the level of profit. They only seek current small profits and do not know how to measure future risks. Risks in the investment world are unavoidable, but precautions must be taken to reduce them. In advance, one should always silently observe the company's financial management, financial situation, market changes, bank operations, stock exchange reports, and political developments, all of which are closely related to invested funds. Investors do not need to be familiar with such specialized courses, but they should also know their basic outline.

(2) Investment and Speculation

The meanings and directions of investment and speculation are fundamentally different. The analysis is as follows:

(1) Investors often try to avoid danger, so the degree of danger can be reduced to a minimum. Speculators seek huge profits, all in the danger of being significant, so that they can sell short and buy long as they please.

(2) Investors hope to receive legitimate income and do not make extra, unreasonable ideas; speculators only want the principal to appreciate and gain more profit, the more the better, the better.

(3) The rate of return on investment is more regular, while speculation has more irregular income.

(4) When investing, buying and selling securities are mostly paid in cash, and the money and goods are immediately settled. Speculators like to short sell and buy more futures.

(5) Investors' buying and selling behavior is entirely based on statistics; speculators do not.

(6) Investors can accurately analyze market conditions and predict the occurrence of changes, while speculators do not value analysis and fear that there will be few changes.

(3) Development of Investment Opportunities

In all countries around the world, whether old or new, and in market conditions, whether prosperous or declining, investors only need to have sufficient funds ready to proceed. The reasons are as follows:

(1) The increase in population and the concentration of rural people in cities has become a common phenomenon in various countries. Therefore, human needs are increasing day by day. The original industries should urgently increase production and expand their organizations, and new enterprises are emerging one after another. All of this requires huge capital to establish their foundations.

(2) The increase in the level of life. The more advanced the society, the richer human life becomes, and the types of consumer goods are constantly changing, and the quality and quantity are different from before. Manufacturers strive to adapt to the trend, and they must raise funds to enrich their content.

(3) The development of emerging countries. Not long after the founding of the country, everything is waiting to be done. The organization of politics is gradually perfected, and economic undertakings must follow. The development of colonies, the construction of agriculture, industry and commerce, the completion of transportation routes, and the extraction of minerals are all good opportunities for investors.

(4) Convenient transportation. The denser the network of lines on the map of inland rivers, inland seas, oceans, continents, aviation, and telegraphs, the larger the quantity of a country's import and export trade, and the closer the exchanges between importers, exporters, and financial institutions, and the more frequent the income and expenditure.

(5) Close international relations. Modern countries all know that the ancient closed-door policy is wrong, and they all pay attention to the strategies of international lending and mutual assistance. Therefore, bonds are issued and sold to foreign markets, or the capital of one country is gathered and invested in the production of other countries. There is communication between countries, and surpluses and deficits are mutually supplemented. International investment has become the central business of modern international relations.

(6) Compilation of commercial statistics. The success of investment lies entirely in accurate and complete predictions. All business cycles, the tightness of silver, and the changes in the market value of securities must be based on the Law of Probability and the Law of Average to project the future. In this way, the current capital investment will have a basis to follow and will not go astray.

Investors should be cautious throughout their lives, think carefully and silently observe, and wait quietly for a good opportunity. Do not let profit prevail and act rashly and risk everything.

(4) The Crisis of Investment

Market situations change unpredictably, and market prices rise and fall in an instant. Sometimes gold is expensive and silver is cheap, and sometimes silver is expensive and gold is cheap. The value of currency is also uncertain. Even if investors can use their intelligence and think carefully before acting, it is sometimes difficult to completely avoid the following risks:

(1) The risk of market price. Securities may increase or decrease, and capital may be more or less. Although there is a law of supply and demand as a guideline, the arrival of political and economic emergencies is rapid and serious, often making it difficult for investors to cope, and eventually leading to failure.

(2) The risk of commercial organization credit. Companies issuing company bonds or stocks often have poor turnover and cannot maintain themselves in the "unfavorable situation". The managers initially try to keep secrets and deceive themselves, but once they declare bankruptcy, it is like a bolt from the blue, harming themselves and others. If investors cannot predict and collect the securities they issue, they will inevitably be harmed.

(3) The risk of political organization credit. Public finances always lead to budget overruns, which cannot be compensated. The original lottery repayment method for public bonds may not be implemented, and market credit will plummet, even if it recovers.

(4) The risk of personnel. Wars, riots, and other events that disrupt social order can cause the stock exchange to stop trading, all industries to decline, and the market to collapse. What about investment? What about safety?

(5) The risk of natural disasters. Earthquakes, floods, hurricanes, volcanic eruptions, and droughts all cause losses to the investment world, which cannot be resisted.

Where there is enterprise, there must be danger. Bank managers are busy signing contracts for securities futures every day, often tossing and turning in their sleep at midnight, all because they are responsible for significant and dangerous situations.

(5) The Cost of Investment Risk

The existence of risk in the investment world is normal, not an abnormal phenomenon. Because there are often risks, there must often be corresponding rewards to compensate for the losses and to reward the mental effort of avoiding risks. In terms of losses, it is like the profit of an entrepreneur, and in terms of mental effort, it is like the wages of a worker, but this reward should not be too high or too low. It should be considered in the middle to find a fair and safe way. The analysis of its composition is as follows:

(1) True Income. The interest on investment cannot be lower than the true income that should be received. If there is no income or the income is too little, investors will hesitate and market will lack capital, so interest rates must increase.

(2) Reasonable Profit. The interest on investment does not have to be higher than a reasonable profit, because businesses that use capital should also have a reasonable profit themselves. Investors who provide capital cannot infringe on this number. Otherwise, businesses will fear the high peak of interest and fear that they will work hard for nothing, and they will also hesitate. In this case, even if investors have capital, they will have few opportunities to release it. Heroes have no place to use their talents, and personal suffering is a small matter. The stagnation of social cash is harmful to industry and commerce. In fact, the interest paid by borrowers to lenders must be lower than the profits that should be earned, and the level of capital interest depends entirely on the earning power of the enterprise. Generally, an annual interest rate of 5% to 1.2% is considered a good standard, and an annual interest rate of 7% or 8% is a moderate and reasonable interest rate. Investors may not care about the safety of the principal, but otherwise this standard is essential. Therefore, since the establishment of the Republic of China, the domestic public bonds issued by the government, except for the special salt surplus treasury bills issued in August of the eleventh year with a monthly interest rate of 2%, the special tobacco and alcohol treasury bills issued in February of the tenth year with a monthly interest rate of 1.5%, and the autumn festival payment treasury bills issued in September of the twelfth year with a monthly interest rate of 1%, the special salt surplus treasury bills issued in May of the same year with a monthly interest rate of 1.5%, the Chongwenmen Jinpu freight donation special treasury bills issued in April of the thirteenth year of the Republic of China with a monthly interest rate of 1%, and the special salt surplus 14 treasury bills issued in January of the eleventh year of the Republic of China with a monthly interest rate of 1.5%, which have higher interest rates, and the financial long-term public bonds of the Ministry of Finance of the National Government in the seventeenth year, which have a particularly low annual interest rate of only 2.5%; in addition, the annual or monthly interest rates of various public bonds and treasury bills are all 6% to 8%.

(6) Rationalized Investment

Recently, countries have been competing to promote the policy of rationalization. All economic behaviors, such as production, consumption, trade, and distribution, have certain positive and perfect norms. Investors should pay attention to the following matters according to this principle:

1. Capital must be invested in productive undertakings. All other unproductive and uneconomic matters, even if the temporary interest is high, should not be moved by it, making reckless investments, and causing future worries.

2. Attention must be paid to the management and operating methods of those who use funds, because if one management is improper, the profit will be reduced, and the loss will be serious, even bankruptcy and closure.

3. The main purpose is to obtain true and reasonable income, and investors should not demand high interest.

4. The risk of enterprises that use funds should not be too great. Investors should be cautious everywhere and avoid risky and fierce opportunities. One must know that if danger occurs, good capital will inevitably be lost.
