Archbishop Tsai Ning, the Roman Catholic Apostolic Delegate to China, departed from Shanghai for Fujian yesterday afternoon at 2:00 PM aboard a sea vessel to inspect Catholic affairs in South China. Archbishop Tsai arrived at the Datong Wharf around 1:00 PM to board the ship. Bishops from various regions came to the dock to see him off. It is expected that after arriving in Fujian, he will visit various dioceses before returning north.

15th Lottery Winning Ticket Holder 88

Da Yun Company Frequently Awards Big Prizes: A Laborer Becomes Wealthy Overnight

Da Yun Company, located at 170 Avenue Edward VII in the French Concession of this city, is the general manager for the sale of aviation highway construction lottery tickets for the six provinces of Zhejiang, Anhui, Jiangxi, Hubei, and Sichuan. Since the first period until the fifteenth period, the company has repeatedly sold first, second, and third prize winning tickets. The first prize ticket for the fifteenth period, number 185371, was sold by Jin Cheng Bank, which was supplied by Da Yun Company. It is reported that the owner is a Taiping Bank employee who bought two tickets, a certain Mr. from Yan Hua Lou bought two tickets, a Shanghai Municipal Council coolie worker bought one ticket, and a Western woman from 141 Seymour Road bought five tickets. The company's retail store sold one second prize and one third prize ticket, and the mail order department sold one second prize ticket and three third prize tickets. It was found that the second prize ticket sent out by the mail order department went to a Mr. Qiu of Xijie, Shaanxi Road, Chongqing, who had five tickets, a Mr. Gu of Xingan, Jiangxi, who had one ticket, and a Mr. Chen of Guyijie, Haozhou, Anhui, who had four tickets. The most amazing thing is that the third prize ticket number 122252 was distributed to the company's retail store on September 12th. Except for the five tickets that were sold sporadically every day, the remaining five tickets were left. All the ticket buyers felt that the word "two" on the ticket was too much and it was not easy to win the prize, and they looked down upon it. Until the draw day, at 11 am, the tickets were sold out, leaving only five of these tickets. A certain gentleman bought them and put them in his wallet without even looking at the numbers. After the lottery was drawn, he won the third prize. This can be said to be a coincidence. The company's retail and mail order departments are overflowing with tickets for the 16th period. This is due to the frequent big prizes and outstanding credibility. Recently, it has been learned that some stores do not care about their reputation and specialize in printing advertisements to deceive people from other places. The methods are fantastic, so don't believe them lightly. You will be fooled. Da Yun Company is the general agency for sales and there are no mistakes.

Lu Chongpeng and Lu Shuyun's Relocation Case: Appeal Changes Judgment, Lu Chongpeng Sentenced to Ten Months with Three Years' Probation 89

Lu Chongpeng, a former congressman from Haimen, now resides at No. 1, Lane 98, Grosvenor Gardens in the French Concession and has been a Shanghai resident for several years. He previously lived at No. 24, Qingyun Lane, Rue Ratard, and due to a rent dispute, he was involved in several lawsuits in the Civil Court of the Special Court with the landlord, Yuan Chang Company. After relocating to Grosvenor Gardens on August 4th of this year, he filed a complaint with the Criminal Court of the Special Court, claiming that the Qingyun Lane landlord Lu Shuyun had obstructed the relocation and damaged antique porcelain. He accused Lu Shuyun of two crimes: restricting freedom and causing damage, and filed a civil suit, requesting a judgment to compensate for the losses. The defendant, Lu Shuyun, also filed a counterclaim for false accusation and obstructing official duties (referring to the plaintiff tearing up the seal during the court's attachment). The initial trial resulted in a judgment that Lu Shuyun was fined twenty yuan and compensated Lu Chongpeng for ten yuan in losses. Lu Chongpeng was found not guilty on the counterclaim. After the judgment was delivered, the defendant Lu Shuyun, dissatisfied with the original judgment, hired lawyer Sun Yuan to file an appeal with the High Court. The plaintiff Lu Chongpeng also appealed, arguing that the original judgment was an inappropriate sentence. Judges Sun Honglin, Wang Tiexiong, and Hui Ping of the High Court held a collegiate hearing on the 24th of last month. Lu Chongpeng did not attend, but Lu Shuyun attended with his defense lawyer. After the hearing, the debate was declared closed, and the date for the judgment was set. These details have already been reported in this newspaper. Now, we learn that the judgment was made the day before yesterday, the main text of which states: the part of the original judgment regarding Lu Shuyun and Lu Chongpeng being not guilty is revoked. Lu Chongpeng, intending to have another person subjected to criminal punishment, made a false accusation to the competent public official and is sentenced to ten months of imprisonment, with a three-year probation. Lu Shuyun is not guilty. Other appeals are rejected. Regarding the incidental civil appeal from both parties, the main text of the judgment states: the part of the original judgment regarding compensation for losses is revoked. Lu Chongpeng's lawsuit and appeal in the first instance are both rejected. It is reported that Lu Chongpeng's side has expressed dissatisfaction with this second instance judgment and has decided to file a third instance appeal with the Supreme Court.

The History Surname Widow-Daughter-in-Law Mutual Lawsuit Case Concluded 90

The young widow Ye Cuiying filed a lawsuit in the civil court of the district court, requesting to be separated from her father-in-law Shi Yongkang. Because Ye Cuiying had accused her father-in-law of misconduct in court, Shi Yongkang accused his daughter-in-law of intentional defamation and damage to his reputation. He accused her of loose morals to the court prosecutor's office. The father-in-law and daughter-in-law slandered each other. As a result, Ye Cuiying was given a non-prosecution disposition. The civil part of the case had previously been heard once, but no conclusion had been reached, as detailed in previous reports. It is now learned that this case was heard again yesterday afternoon at 4:00 PM by Judge Han Jingji in the second court. Ye Cuiying still attended court with her lawyer Hu Yuanjun and made a statement. Next, Wang Baofeng, the owner of the Wang Dou Ji store, testified that regarding the widow residing in the Shi Yongkang family next door, he and Shi Yongkang, due to their fellow-villager relationship, had advised her to live with her mother-in-law to avoid gossip. Unexpectedly, Shi held a grudge and accused him of having an improper relationship with his daughter-in-law, which was a false accusation. As for giving her stomach medicine, it was medicine left over from his wife's use. The presiding judge then questioned Shi Yongkang for a few words. Since the case was clear, the debate was declared over, and the judgment was scheduled to be pronounced at 2:00 PM on the fifth.

Municipal Chamber of Commerce Decides to Handle the Shanghai Guohuo Company Amicable Settlement Case; Appoints Ke Ganchen and Xu Yongzuo to Review the Books 91

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce previously received a letter from the liquidators of Shanghai Guohuo Co., Ltd. - Hong Yanbin, Wang Jian, Zhang Zilian, Zou Xingsan, Zhang Henghai, etc. - stating that the company's asset-liability situation showed clear signs of being unable to repay debts. In accordance with the provisions of Article 41 of the Bankruptcy Law, they applied for an amicable settlement. After receiving a letter from the company's liquidators confirming that the company's creditors had not applied to the court for bankruptcy, the association submitted it to the 65th Standing Committee meeting for discussion and decided to accept the company's liquidators' application for amicable settlement. A letter was sent to the liquidators, requesting them to submit the books and plans that should be prepared in accordance with Article 7 of the same law. On the 31st of this month, the liquidators submitted the Shanghai Guohuo Company's balance sheet, list of creditors, list of debtors, and amicable settlement plan to the association. It was then submitted to the 67th Standing Committee meeting for discussion and decision to appoint Standing Committee member Ke Ganchen and accountant Xu Yongzuo to review the various books and handle this amicable settlement case. It is reported that the association has sent separate letters to Standing Committee member Ke Ganchen and accountant Xu Yongzuo to jointly handle the matter.

Candle Industry Receives Approval from Ministry of Finance to Prohibit Superstitious Donations in Fujian Province 92

The Candle Industry Guild previously reported that the Fujian Provincial Government was planning to implement a special tax on superstition, with an extremely heavy tax rate, fearing that it would have ramifications. They immediately telegraphed the Ministry of Finance in Nanjing, appealing for an investigation and a request for prohibition. Now, they have received a decree from the Ministry of Finance, No. 7654, which states, "Your telegram has been received. Whether there is such a proposal in the province has not been reported to the Ministry for the record. Regarding the previous situation, we have already consulted the Fujian Provincial Government to investigate and order a halt. Please take note." After receiving this decree, the guild immediately copied and issued the original decree, notifying the industry colleagues in this city and other locations separately.
